Accomplice in Assassination Case, Gu Qingbao, Arrested 139

Detective Bureau Reports the Incident of Jiang Guoxing's Death

Gu Was Present at the Scene and Was Also a Conspirator

On the afternoon of January 29th last year at 5:30 PM, an assassination case occurred at Yuanfang Lane, Huaji Road, Hongkou. The deceased was named Jiang Guoxing, who specialized in being an informant. If he learned that there were contraband items somewhere, he would report to the police or detectives, which led to him being resented by others and assassinated. After the incident, the police arrested the perpetrators Gu Hairu, Ge Xiaosuo, Ji Xiaobao, Miao Zuobi, Mizukami Ko, and others, and sent them to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Gu and others confessed that there was also a co-conspirator in this case, Gu Qingbao (also known as Gu Aqing or Chen Aqing), who was at large. As a result, Gu Hairu was sentenced to life imprisonment, Ge Xiaosuo was sentenced to death, and the others were also punished separately. Later, Gu and Ge declared that they were not convinced and filed an appeal. After the Court of Appeal changed the sentence to 15 years for Gu and life imprisonment for Ge, they were sent to prison for execution. At the same time, the police reported to the court and obtained an arrest warrant for Gu. Two years have passed since the incident, and until yesterday afternoon, the Chinese detective of the Putuo Road Police Station learned that Gu Qingbao had returned to Shanghai and was currently eating at a restaurant in Xuejia浜, Limadu, Nanshi. They then joined the police detectives of the Nanshi Public Security Bureau to arrest Gu Qingbao and take him back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court and charged with premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Code. According to the Detective Bureau lawyer Zhang Tianyin, who stood up and stated the case, after Jiang Guoxing was killed, the police arrested the perpetrators Gu Hairu, Ge Xiaosuo, and others. According to Gu's previous confession at the police station, in detail, he said that at that time, in addition to him, there were Ge Xiaosuo, Chen Dacheng, and Gu Qingbao, who were waiting in Yuanfang Lane. When they saw Jiang passing by, Chen and Ge suddenly stepped forward and first knocked Jiang down with their fists. Ge then chopped him several times with a sharp axe, but Jiang still did not die. Therefore, Chen Dacheng opened fire on him twice with a pistol, and Chen also fired one shot. Jiang then died. The defendant in this case, Gu Qingbao, in addition to being at the scene at the time, was also a co-conspirator in the prior discussion. There is also a witness, He Jiaji, who was at the scene when the incident occurred. He can prove that the defendant Gu Qingbao was the first to shout "Hit!" "Hit!" Chen and Ge then immediately took action. The Detective Bureau detectives went to He's house at No. 14 Yuanfang Lane, Huaji Road, yesterday to inquire, but He was out. They instructed his father to inform He Jiaji to appear in court today to testify, but it is suspected that he was threatened by the defendant and dared not appear in court. Therefore, the court is requested to issue a ticket ordering him to be summoned. Moreover, the Detective Bureau still needs to investigate evidence in this case, and the trial should be adjourned. Then, Jiang Lu, the wife of the victim, and He Jiaji's father reported the case and testified. When questioned, the defendant denied that he had conspired to commit murder. He only claimed that Jiang Guoxing had always known him and hated him. Since Jiang was killed, because there was a Western detective from the police station investigating at his home, he dared not go back and went to Chongqing to do business. After returning to Shanghai, he still lived in his home at No. 43 Yuanfang Lane. He hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him. Judge Liu Yugui reviewed the confession and ordered Gu to be detained for further investigation in seven days.

The case regarding the reconsideration of Article 239 of the Criminal Code, which has attracted social attention, was resolved by the Legislative Yuan at its regular meeting on the 23rd to be submitted to the Criminal Law Committee and the Legal System Committee for review. It is reported that the Chinese Women's Movement League, the Shanghai Women's Advancement Association, the Chinese Women's Temperance Association, and the Chinese Women's Society of this city believe that the Legislative Yuan intends to delay the matter. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, they convened a joint emergency meeting and resolved to send representatives to unite women from various regions, organize an expanded petition group, appeal to the capital, and re-issue a circular telegram to women's groups and female compatriots across the country. The original text is as follows:

To all national women's groups, female schools, and 200 million female compatriots: We hereby inform you that the amendment to Article 239 of the Criminal Code has already been resolved by the Central Political Council and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for reconsideration. Our women's groups have repeatedly submitted petitions stating the reasons in the past. Unexpectedly, at the Legislative Yuan's regular meeting this Friday, it was decided to use the delaying tactic of submitting it for review and shelving it. The news of this has caused us great consternation. How can such a law that violates the teachings of the late Premier and overturns the prestige of the New Life Movement be allowed to exist under the banner of the Blue Sky with a White Sun? Our associations, etc., have decided to immediately send representatives to various cities and counties across the country to jointly organize a petition group, travel to the capital as quickly as possible, and expand the movement. Our female compatriots should immediately rise up in unison, redouble their efforts, and with a resolute spirit and orderly steps, vow to fight to the death to eliminate this feudal legacy. We will never give up until our goal is achieved. The time is pressing, and there is no time to delay. This is a one-time opportunity. Please be aware of this. Chinese Women's Movement League, Shanghai Women's Advancement Association, Chinese Women's Society, Chinese Women's Temperance Association.

Regulations for Land Leasing in the Central Urban Administrative District 141

Announced by the Municipal Government

The municipal government hereby announces the regulations for land leasing in the central urban administrative district of Shanghai. The original text is as follows: (Article 1) When government agencies, state-owned enterprises, organizations, or private individuals need land to construct the following types of buildings, they may apply to the municipal government to lease part of the public land within the central urban administrative district that is not needed by the municipal government itself, in accordance with the regulations on the handling of public land: A. Office buildings for government agencies or state-owned enterprises; B. Libraries, museums, or other exhibition venues related to culture and education. (Article 2) When government agencies or state-owned enterprises request to lease public land, they shall submit architectural drawings and proof that the construction funds for the project have been approved by higher-level authorities. When organizations or private individuals request to lease public land, they shall submit a project plan and architectural drawings, and have secured more than half of the construction funds for the project, with a reliable bank guarantee. (Article 3) The term and rent for leasing public land shall be handled in accordance with the regulations on the handling of public land. The area and location of the leased public land shall be determined by the municipal government. (Article 4) Leased public land shall not be subleased. (Article 5) Unless there are special circumstances approved by the municipal government, construction must commence within one year after the lease is determined and completed within three years. (Article 6) The use of the buildings on the leased public land shall not violate the provisions of Article 1 of these regulations. (Article 7) If it is desired to continue leasing after the expiration of the lease term, a new application shall be submitted to the municipal government in accordance with these regulations three months in advance. (Article 8) If the provisions of Articles 4 to 6 of these regulations are violated, the municipal government may recover the leased land. (Article 9) If the buildings on the public land are not demolished immediately after the expiration of the lease term and the lease is not continued, the municipal government may appropriately take them over or order their demolition within a time limit. (Article 10) All contractual matters related to the leasing of public land shall be handled by the responsible bureau. (Article 11) These regulations may be amended at any time if there are any omissions. (Article 12) These regulations shall come into effect from the date of promulgation.

French Female Pianist Comes to Shanghai 142

The French female pianist, Madame René Florigny, is endowed with musical genius and is renowned throughout the world, earning her the title of a female Paderewski. (Note: Paderewski was a famous Polish musician, composer, and statesman who served as the President and Minister of Foreign Affairs of the Republic of Poland in 1919.) Madame Florigny's artistry is extraordinary, and she admires Chinese culture. She is determined to promote the exchange of Chinese and Western music. This is her first time coming to China, and the upcoming event is expected to be a grand occasion.

New Pharmaceutical Association's Measures for Members Being Falsely Accused 144

Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The New Pharmaceutical Industry Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: Our association member, Shi Zhifu, of Wan Guo Pharmacy, etc., was falsely accused by Ma Wu Jiu, etc., of privately manufacturing red pills. The Public Security Bureau detained him and sent him to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters. Now, because the chemical test results of the confiscated drugs show that there are no toxic substances, he has been released. However, he was innocently imprisoned for more than two weeks, which has greatly affected his business. Therefore, an extraordinary meeting of member representatives was convened to discuss the matter. It was unanimously believed that being detained without being allowed bail after being falsely accused is too insecure. It was resolved that the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce should be requested to forward a request to the municipal government, urging it to instruct the Public Security and Health Bureaus to recognize those who have obtained a pharmaceutical merchant license from the Health Bureau as legitimate pharmacies in the future when such unexpected events occur, and allow the association to provide guarantees to avoid innocent people from being implicated. We are hereby recording this case and forwarding it to you. Please grant us permission to forward it.

Notes on the Personnel Management Association's Speech 145

In order to promote the study of personnel management issues, the Personnel Management Association stipulates that a lecture meeting will be held once a month, inviting experts to give lectures. It is learned that the association held its second lecture meeting yesterday at the YMCA in Eight Immortals Bridge, inviting Mr. Huang Renzhi, director of the China Vocational Education Society and general secretary of the Shanghai Local Association, to speak on the issue of "How to Prevent Embezzlement by Industrial and Commercial Employees." More than 60 directors, members, and students of the training institute attended. First, Dr. He Qingru delivered the opening speech, followed by Mr. Huang's speech. The main points of his speech were: (1) Preventing embezzlement from a business perspective is not as effective as preventing it from outside the business. Individual conversations and attention to leisure issues can be utilized. (2) Relying on leaders' speeches to prevent embezzlement is not as effective as relying on colleagues' mutual admonitions. Pay attention to the friends with whom employees associate and strictly control small group organizations. (3) Relying on rules and regulations to prevent embezzlement is not as effective as relying on personal influence. Leaders must set an example in every word and deed, etc. His words were weighty, pertinent, and practical, truly a product of experience. The listeners benefited greatly.

New Trick for Swindling Pewter Wine Pots 151

Wang Awei Scammed More Than 500

Owner of the receiving shop and four others detained

Wang Awei, a rogue, 28 years old, from Ningbo, recently had a far-fetched idea and roamed the streets, falsely claiming to be a resident of a certain number on a certain road to large and small hotels in the city, and requested that several catties of Shaoxing wine be delivered immediately. The hotels, because the customers were coming to their door, all agreed and immediately sent their staff to deliver the Shaoxing wine they wanted in pewter wine pots to the designated location. Unexpectedly, Wang was already standing at the doorstep of his so-called house number. When he saw the wine staff coming, he immediately greeted them and said, "I still need several catties of Shaoxing wine now. Please go back to the shop and bring it to add to the Shaoxing wine you brought, and you can give it to me to take inside. Hurry, don't delay," etc. At this time, the wine staff did not suspect him of fraud, so they all handed over the wine pots they were carrying to Wang to take inside, and returned to the shop to add more wine. Unexpectedly, when they brought the wine for the second time, Wang had already fled without a trace. When they asked the residents, they all said that they had not sent anyone to call for wine. At this point, the wine staff realized that they had been deceived. They immediately returned to the shop and reported to their master, to no avail. Moreover, because Wang's scam was ingenious, the number of hotels in the city that had been deceived by him had reached hundreds, and Wang had successively scammed more than 500 pewter wine pots, which he sold cheaply to Wan Tai Copper and Tin, etc., at No. 1657 Fangbang Road to melt down into pewterware. As for the Shaoxing wine, it was all sold to rickshaw pullers for drinking. Wang made a great profit, so he made a living from it. Unexpectedly, at around 10 a.m. yesterday, Wang went to a certain place again and scammed two wine pots. When he passed near Fangbang Bridge, he was suddenly discovered by Chen Caifu, Dong Wenrui, leaders of the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and detectives Zhao Huai'ren, Li Ruizhi, etc., who were patrolling. They searched him and found the stolen goods, and took him back to the team. Captain Lu interrogated him and learned the whole story. He immediately sent Chen and others to Wan Tai, Yuan Yuan, Yuan Yichang, and other copper and tin shops to recover dozens of stolen pewter wine pots, and detained four people: Lu Deyou, owner of Wan Tai, Li Zhifang, a shop assistant, Wang Yueting, owner of Yuan Yuan, and Yuan Yiji, owner of Yuan Yichang. They were all taken to the team and sent to the bureau for interrogation.

The Past Love and Separation of Lin Yujin and Sheng Yuchang 152

Lin was first a prostitute and then a dancer

Reunited after separation, then abandoned again

Sheng Yuchang, 38 years old this year, the eldest grandson of Sheng Xingsun, former Qing Dynasty Grand Guardian and Minister of Posts and Communications, from Changzhou, resides at No. 1 Avenue Petain in the French Concession. He previously lived with Yan Shuangqin, the second daughter of Yan Minghan, a local Taoist priest living on Kang Nao Road in West Shanghai, due to love. Later, because the woman's brother-in-law, Zheng Shifan, was involved in a kidnapping case and arrested, the two people's feelings broke down and they separated. The woman's parents, as legal representatives, accompanied the woman and hired a lawyer to sue Sheng Yuchang for abandonment in the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. After several summonses, Sheng finally agreed to an unconditional reconciliation on July 26 of last year, restored the old relationship, and lived together again. The case was then closed. Recently, a Guangdong woman, Lin Yujin (27 years old this year, residing at No. 16 Renzhi Lane, North Sichuan Road), hired a lawyer and filed a complaint in the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court accusing Sheng Yuchang of abandonment. The court, according to the complaint, scheduled a summons for all parties yesterday, as was briefly recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Here is a supplementary record of the intention and reasons for the prosecution. Lin Yujin was a prostitute in Changsan Shuyu in her early years, under the name Xin Yujin. At the age of 16, she was introduced by Su Shichi and married Sheng Yuchang as a concubine, the fourth concubine. They lived together in Zhabei Wuzhen Road, Seymour Road Baochang Lane, etc. They got along for two years. Because Sheng kept many concubines and was not devoted to his affections, he initially doted on Miss Lin, but then listened to the slander of other concubines and treated her cruelly, punching and kicking her as usual. Sheng then forced her to sign a statement of disassociation and drove her out of the house without giving her a penny. Miss Lin sighed at her misfortune and did not want to argue with him, so she left and became a dancer in a Shanghai dance hall to make a living. Unexpectedly, she met Sheng again in the dance hall. Sheng, seeing Miss Lin hugging and dancing with others, was concerned about his reputation, so he called Miss Lin to him, gave her 200 yuan, and told her not to work as a dancer in the future, and promised to give her 300 yuan a month for living expenses from then on. Since then, Lin Yujin lived with Sheng again, renting a house at No. 291 Renhe Lane, Avenue Joffre, upstairs from the Jinhua Pharmacy. Lin was overjoyed to have found someone to rely on for the rest of her life. However, Lin suffered from lung disease, and Sheng, although he had a heart of love, was afraid of contracting lung disease, so he gradually became cold towards her again. From April of this year, he stopped providing living expenses and abandoned her. Lin visited him several times, but it was difficult to see him because Sheng's residence was like a sea. At this point, Lin believed that Sheng had deliberately abandoned her, so she filed a complaint, requesting that he be interrogated in accordance with Article 310 of the Criminal Code, and also filed a civil lawsuit, requesting that he be ordered to pay 50,000 yuan in alimony. The court, according to the complaint, issued a summons and sent a police officer to deliver it to the defendant. His family replied that Sheng was in Hangzhou, so they refused to accept the summons. At 10 a.m. yesterday, Judge Xiong Huiping and clerk Zheng Rong arrived at the Sixth Court for trial. The defendant did not appoint a lawyer to attend on his behalf, only the plaintiff Lin Yujin and her lawyer attended. After briefly stating the case, the judge announced the reason why the defendant had not been summoned, and then the plaintiff's lawyer stated that since the defendant had not attended today, he requested that an arrest warrant be issued to arrest him. The court ordered a postponement of the hearing until the defendant was summoned.

Crackdown on Golden Rooster Red Treasure Pills 153

Tested and Found to be Made of Morphine, etc.

Owner of Ziqiang Company on the Run

The China Ziqiang Pharmaceutical Company was established at No. 13 Ci Zhuan Lane, West Lin Road, outside Ximen. Its owner, Wang Dianrong, had a large internal organization and scale, and specialized in manufacturing Golden Rooster Lingbao Pills (i.e., Ningbao Pills), a variant of red pills for quitting opium. It had been open for nearly a year. The Municipal Public Security Bureau received a confidential report stating that these Golden Rooster Lingbao Pills were a variant of red pills, and that the raw materials used were made of morphine and other toxic substances. Because red pills had been severely banned recently, these Lingbao Pills were widely sold and had branch distribution centers at No. 4, opposite the Xiyuan Bathhouse at the entrance of Chun De Lane, Avenue Lamwe, French Concession, and at the Mafa Ji of Cao Xie Bang, Little Shaodu Road, Avenue Robert. They were distributed to Chongming, Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, Huzhou, Nanjing, Wuhu, Hankou, Jiujiang, Anqing, Changsha, Shandong, Tianjin, Peiping, Qingdao, and other places outside the city. After receiving the confidential report, the Public Security Bureau sent personnel to purchase several packages (large packages sold for 50 cents, small packages sold for 10 cents) and submitted them to the Municipal Government for transfer to the Health Department for testing. The results confirmed that they were made of morphine and other toxic substances. They were sold everywhere, poisoning people. Therefore, the Municipal Public Security Bureau immediately secretly ordered Lu Ying, the captain of the detective team, to order Shen Wenda and Fang Linggen, the detective team leaders stationed in the Ximen branch, and detectives Zheng Yongxiang, Bian Wenqing, Jiao Baojun, Yu Wenhai, and Liu Wenhui, to work with patrol officer He and police officers to secretly go to the above-mentioned locations at 5:30 p.m. yesterday. On the spot, a large number of Golden Rooster Lingbao Pills, weighing 12 catties, as well as printing boxes, wooden boards, and other items were seized. Wang Ni Shi, 21 years old, from Nanjing, residing at No. 13 Ci Hui Lane (i.e., Wang Dianrong's wife), Ma Miao Gen, 51 years old, local, residing at the same address, Sun Yi Bao, 53 years old, from Huzhou, residing at the same address, and Wang Shunrong, 30 years old, from Nanjing, residing at No. 10 Xujiahui Road, were arrested. The main suspect, Wang Dianrong, was on the run and has not been caught. The detective team leaders Shen Wenda, etc., took the people and stolen goods to the Ximen branch, where the branch director, Police Officer Li, briefly interrogated them. Because the matter was a strict order from the higher authorities, he immediately prepared a document to send them to the general bureau for interrogation.

At around 3 p.m. the day before yesterday, Sang Zhichuan, a native of Ningbo, went to No. 22 Xinxing Lane, Huasheng Road, Zhabei, and found his runaway concubine, Sang Cheng Shi, and dragged her to the Xinzha Public Security Bureau. Later, she worked as a nurse at the Guangdong Children's and Disabled Hospital (now renamed Zhongshan Hospital). Later, he moved her back to his home at No. 58 Changyun Lane, Dagu Road. Unexpectedly, he still had an old wife and four daughters-in-law at home, who drove her out. So she temporarily lived in the Dahua Apartments. From then on, he treated her worse and often beat and insulted her. Later, when she went out, he took all her clothes and passbooks, totaling more than 1,000 yuan, which she had brought from Guangdong. Since then, she has been wandering around and gave birth to a child named Pinwei on May 23 of this year. She is currently staying at her maternal uncle Wang Jinsheng's place, bringing the case, etc. After the interrogating officer verified the confession, he ruled that the case was complicated and sent it to the Judicial Section of Zhabei. She was escorted to the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau for disposition at around 10 a.m. yesterday.

French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Union Strictly Prevents Fraudulent Fee Collection 162

According to a tip-off from members of the Shanghai Second District Water and Electricity Industry Union (i.e., the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Union), recently, unscrupulous individuals have been impersonating the union to collect introduction fees and large membership fees under the pretext of introducing jobs at the French Concession Water and Electricity Company. The union convened an emergency meeting of the board of directors and supervisors on the 21st of this month. It was unanimously agreed that the French Concession Water and Electricity Company never charges a fee for hiring workers. The union's usual practice for membership application is to collect a membership fee of one yuan in accordance with the Trade Union Law and the union's charter, but it must be certified by the group leader of the respective group and introduced by two or more members of the union. Membership is only granted after review and approval by the board of directors. It is outrageous that unscrupulous individuals dare to damage the union's reputation and deceive society. If this is not thoroughly investigated, it will seriously harm the union's reputation in the future. It was decided to prepare a document and send it to the party and government authorities, and forward it to the Huazu police authorities, to strictly arrest such unscrupulous individuals. At the same time, an urgent notice was issued to all members and workers to be vigilant. If such incidents are discovered, they should be handed over to the police authorities and transferred to the judicial organs for severe punishment according to law, in order to deter evildoers and maintain the union's reputation.

Three Kidnappers Executed 163

Numerous Crimes and Heinous Offenses Exposed

Silent at Death, But Asked for Ghost Money

The notorious kidnappers Zhang Er'a (28 years old, formerly a chauffeur), Yu Afu (25 years old, formerly a cart puller), and Ding Zinan (28 years old, unemployed vagrant) were all from Tongzhou. On April 3, 1929, at 7 pm, they, along with accomplices Zhang Qishan, Tang Yongshun, Xi Houtao, Tang Rongzong, Tang Yongfu, etc., kidnapped Deng Zhonghe outside No. 378 Ningbo Road and demanded ransom. At that time, they immediately tied Deng up and took him to a祠堂 (ancestral hall) in Pudong, hiding him in the loft. Zhang Er'a and others took turns guarding him for more than ten days and then divided the ransom of 120 yuan. Later, Zhang Er'a, Yu Afu, Tang Yongshun, and Qian Xu'en, Ji Jinhua, Wang Alin, etc., who had already been executed by firing squad, kidnapped Liu Tongsheng outside No. 218 Yuezhou Road at about 10 am on July 6, 1932, and demanded ransom. Zhang Er'a stood at the intersection of Zhoushan Road as a lookout while Liu was being kidnapped. When the car arrived at Tangjia浜 (Tang Family Creek), it ran out of gasoline. Qian Xu'en and others then took Liu Tongsheng out of the car. He was rescued by the local defense corps, and Tang Yongshun and other bandits fled in all directions. In December of the same year, Zhang Er'a, Yu Afu, Ding Zinan, Wu Er'a, Tang Yongfu, and Cao Houfu, Zhao Lian, Lao Wang, Xiao Dongyang, etc., who were at large, discussed kidnapping Fang Jinhong of the Sincere Company at the Deyilou in the Eight Immortals Bridge area and demanding ransom. Lao Wang was responsible for hiring the car, Wu Er'a was responsible for driving the car, and Cao Houfu was responsible for advancing the money. First, Zhang Qishan, Xi Houtao, and Cao Houfu, through the rickshaw puller Qian Hengshan, pointed out Fang Jinming at the entrance of the Sincere Company, and Cao Houfu identified the location for hiding the ransom note at the祠堂 (ancestral hall) on Lincoln Road. Tang Yongshun and Xiao Bai and Xiao Da waited there to collect the note. Cao Houfu did not have money to advance, so Tang Rongzong advanced 5 yuan to Ding Zinan and 10 yuan to Tang Yongfu. Then, at about 7 pm on December 9, when Fang Jinming was returning home, they implemented the kidnapping plan. First, Cao Houfu, Zhang Qishan, and Wu Houtao invited Qian Hengshan to the north side of the Sincere Company. Cao Houfu ordered Xi Houtao to follow Fang Jinming on the tram at the entrance of the Sincere Company. At the Jing'an Temple Road station, Fang Jinming transferred to a trackless trolley. Cao Houfu followed him to Yuyuan Road. At that time, Tang Yongfu was riding a bicycle, acting as a lookout in the Yuyuan Road area. Lao Wang hired a car from the Tiantian Motor Company on Baker Road. The chauffeur, Deng Jinsheng, drove to the east side of Yuyuan Road, at the bamboo fence alley entrance on Yidingpan Road. Lao Wang threatened him with a gun and drove Deng Jinsheng out of the car, sending him into the alley to be guarded by Yu Afu. Lao Wang returned to the car, and Wu Er'a drove. Zhang Er'a, Zhao Da, and Ding Zinan got into the car one after another and drove to the Zhaofeng Garden area on Yuyuan Road. Because Fang was stubborn and shouted, he provoked Lao Wang's anger, who shot and killed Fang. Subsequently, the foreign patrol房 (police station) arrested the above three major criminal suspects, Zhang Er'a, Yu Afu, Ding Zinan, Tang Yongshun, Zhang Qishan, Xi Houtao, Tang Rongzong, Tang Yongfu, etc., and handed them over to the First Special District Court. Judge Wu Tingqi repeatedly held court hearings and, after clear investigation, sentenced the three criminals, Zhang Er'a, Yu Afu, and Ding Zinan, to death. (Tang Yongshun, Zhang Qishan, etc., were sentenced to life imprisonment or first-class imprisonment). The judgment was submitted to the superior for review and approval and executed according to the judgment. At about 9 am yesterday, Judge Wu Tingqi of the First Special District Court opened court and ordered the three criminals, Zhang Er'a (i.e., Zhang Mahou), Yu Afu, and Ding Zinan, to be brought to the case. After briefly questioning them and asking if they had any last words, he ordered Chinese and foreign detectives to take the judgment and photos of the criminals and escort them to the Caoh河 (Cao River) and泾 (Jing River) Jiangsu Second Prison for execution. Prior to this, the Special District Court sent a letter to the Nanshi District Court, requesting them to send personnel to supervise. Chief Prosecutor Zhong Shangbin appointed Prosecutor Xie Lian as the supervising execution officer. He also instructed Judicial Sergeant Chen Junfang and Police Inspector Chen Xihui to supervise the execution. Court police officers Wang Jianqing, Zhou Qiwen, Zhang Chunshen, Gao Jinsheng, Xiong Dingchen, Zou Zhendong, Lu Conghe, Zhu Zhiqi, Lu Yin, Shen Tingfang, and Long Zelin took a car to the prison. Soon, the prison cars arrived one after another. Prosecutor Xie Lian ascended to the public case and ordered the three criminals, Zhang Er'a, Yu Afu, and Ding Zinan, to be brought to the case. As usual, he asked about their age, origin, and if they had any last words. The criminals all replied that they had already stated their final wishes to the Special Court, and there was no need to say more. However, they had a request: the Yin and Yang worlds are one. The Yang world needs money, and the Yin world also needs ghost money. Could they buy a one-yuan ghost money ingot? They would be very grateful. They also said that it was only right that they were being executed today. "You reap what you sow, but we don't know how we will be executed. Will it be by shooting or hanging?" The executioner replied that it would be by shooting. The criminals looked at each other and laughed, and said to the executioner, "Please do your job cleanly and quickly. We were all together in life, and we won't be lonely in the underworld after death." After speaking, they strode to the execution ground, knelt side by side. Sergeant Chen Junfang blew a whistle, and three shots were fired simultaneously. The heinous kidnappers fell to the ground and died at the same time. Prosecutor Xie inspected them closely, and Inspector Xuan Zhiming inspected them separately. The bodies were placed in coffins by the court.

Letter 173

To the Editor: I read a news item in yesterday's newspaper about a fire on North Zhejiang Road, which is slightly inconsistent with the facts. I hope you will correct it as follows: "At 5 pm on the 22nd of this month, a fire suddenly broke out in the engine room of a printing factory at No. 5, Lane 138, Houyu里 (Houyu Lane), North Zhejiang Road, where machine oil,格司林 (gasoline), and paper were piled up. The engine room was only separated from our factory by one board. After being discovered by our factory workers, they immediately sounded the alarm and notified the Central Fire Brigade for assistance. However, at that time, the internal water pipes were being repaired due to the main valve, and the water source was cut off, making it impossible to rescue. For a while, the fire was fierce, spreading from the north side of the building to the south side. All of our factory's machinery and buildings were buried in the fire. Later, the Central Fire Brigade drove to the scene and tried their best to put out the fire. According to statistics, the loss suffered by our factory in this disaster is estimated to be more than 50,000 yuan, and more than 80 workers have lost their jobs." This is to the chief editor of the *Shen Bao*, Chen Qingjian, manager of Jinchang Iron Works, November 24th. To the Editorial Department of the *Shen Bao*: Today's local news in your newspaper reported on the Changzhou National Goods Exhibition sponsored by the Association for the Promotion of National Goods, stating that the registration office is located at the first house in Tongan里 (Tongan Lane), across from the Silk Industry Bank on Sanmalu (Third Road), the Preparatory Office of the Changzhou National Exhibition. After investigation, the first house in Tongan里 (Tongan Lane) is our association's office. Although there are vacant rooms for rent on the second and third floors, there is no establishment of the Association for the Promotion of National Goods, nor is there an attached Preparatory Office of the Changzhou National Goods Exhibition. Our association has not been involved in this matter. Because of the reported location, several people have come to ask today, and there may be a misunderstanding. Therefore, we make this statement, and hope that it will be published as a letter to the editor. This is addressed to the Editorial Department of the *Shen Bao*, Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation, 24th.

13 Miles and 800 Meters Public Race Walk to be Held This Morning 176

Starting at 8 AM at the Intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Tongfu Road

78 Male Participants from Four Groups

39 Women to Compete on the Shenyuan Racetrack

The 4th Public Race Walk and the 3rd Women's Race Walk, organized by the China Race Walking Association, are scheduled to be held this morning. The men will start at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Tongfu Road, while the women will compete at the athletic field in Shenyuan. There are 78 male participants, including four team entries: Meteor, Chenguang, Sanduo, and Navy, Army, and Air Force. There are 39 female participants. The men's course is a total of 13 miles and 800 meters. Roll call will be at the Tongfu Road intersection meeting point at 7:45 am, and the race will start with a gunshot at 8:00 am sharp. With a large number of participants, there will be a competition.

Race Walk Route: Via Jing'an Temple Road, Avenue Haig (Jixi Feier Road), to Wujiaochang, enter Route de Sayons (Bailinan Road), cross the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, to Zhoujiaqiao, turn into Route Hoberlan (Hualun Road), Hongqiao Road, cross Avenue Haig, go straight into Route D'astride (Taiside Road), turn onto Bishop Yao Road, Route Petain, Avenue Lafayette, Avenue d'Alber, cross Avenue Foch, to Seymour Road, turn into Xinzha Road, Jiaozhou Road, Connaught Road, to Yanping Road, go straight into the Shenyuan Athletic Field, then walk one lap around the track to finish, a total of 13 miles and 800 meters. The women's competitors will compete in the Shenyuan Athletic Field, walking six laps around the track, totaling 1.5 miles. Roll call will be at 10:50 am, the race will start at 11:00 am, and the awards will be given at 11:30 am.

Numerous Prizes: This competition has received widespread praise and generous donations of prizes from all walks of life. There are already more than 30 prizes from Secretary-General Chu of the Executive Yuan, Mayor Wu, Director Yang, and Supervisor Tang, etc. Yesterday, a dozen coats were sent by the Xie興 (Xie Xing) Sports Equipment Factory, 10 copies of the *Sports Monthly* from the Qinfen Bookstore, and a prize flag from the Juvenile Supplies Supply Company. The prizes are numerous and beautiful. In order to encourage the athletes and increase interest, the China Race Walking Association will give each male athlete who completes the entire course within the stipulated time and each female athlete who completes six laps a commemorative badge from the association's president. The top 30 men and the top 10 women will also receive generous prizes. The entire course is 13 and a half miles long, and every mile will have two Boy Scouts standing with flags to indicate the mileage to help the athletes compete. Regarding traffic, in addition to requesting the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the British and French Concession authorities to dispatch police officers to take care of the route, the Shanghai Municipal Council of the China Boy Scouts Association has also been requested to send about 500 members from Guangyi, Guangzhao, Yucai, Moore Hall, Fudan Middle School, Zhengshi Middle School, Private Shangzhong, YMCA, Yousheng, Jinrong, Minghui, YMCA Middle School, etc., with Wang Gang as the general commander, to assist in everything. At that time, Mr. Ajac, a Westerner, will provide milk, biscuits, and bread to comfort the male and female athletes, and his enthusiasm for sports is admirable. Those大会 (general assembly) staff members who have not yet received ribbons and passes should contact Lu Yutian immediately to get them. Also, today the audience in Shenyuan is bound to be crowded, and in order to limit the number, it will be necessary to charge a small admission fee. It is said that each ticket will only cost 20 cents.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

"Planning" and "Realization" 195

— Feng Ping

Everyone has plans, but plans are either big or small. Big plans concern the conduct of national administration, while small plans concern personal matters. However, various plans may not necessarily be realized.

My younger brother is now studying at a primary school. In the past, every time the semester ended, whether it was the summer or winter vacation, he would always make a plan regarding the subjects he would study on his own during the vacation, and he would also make a very strict timetable. It was indeed a perfect plan, but his plan was never realized.

The reason for his failure is as follows: because he felt very tired mentally after the exams, he took the first week of the vacation as a rest. But in the second week, he changed his tone and said, "There are two months of vacation, why rush so much! It's okay to play for a few days before starting." However, time passed like an arrow, and a week before school started, he felt a little anxious, so he hastily did all the homework! It's just that it's really impossible to put away a heart that has been set free for a long time, so his plans have never been realized year after year.

Children; I'm afraid you have this problem too!

There are two reasons why plans cannot be realized: (1) The plan is too big, and it feels a little difficult to handle; (2) Not starting immediately; You must know that plans can be smaller, but you must use all your energy to do them, and the result will always be a day of realization.

Children: There is nothing in the world that cannot be done well, as long as you work hard! Children! Work hard! Work hard!

Darwin 196

— Zhen

Children, do you know this great man? He was a British naturalist and the originator of the theory of evolution. He was born in 1809 AD and died in 1882 AD, living to the age of 73. His life's deeds can serve as a model for you.

His body was very large, but not very strong. Therefore, he had certain rules for every move he made: he got up at 6:00 AM, and after getting up, he had to take a cold shower, and then walk, read, and do morning exercises in a very quiet place, and work at 8:00 PM.

His method of reading was very scientific. Every time he read a book, he would write the good parts of the book on the last page of the book. If it was someone else's book, he would extract its key points. If he wanted to study a certain subject, he would check the last page of the book and create a new table of the collected information related to that subject. Therefore, all the facts he obtained in his life can be checked one by one without omission.

He was not very precise in dissection, and he could not draw, so it took him more effort than others when he studied, but he encouraged himself and finally achieved good results.

Every time he read a book, he had to think for a long time before he could distinguish what was right and what was wrong. He had a very strong memory. Although he got some general information, he was able to study the materials he had seen before from this general information.

When he was researching and discussing, he was not stubborn about his original opinions at all. Although the theory he had obtained before could solve the facts that he already knew; however, when he was studying the remaining parts, if the theory did not match the new facts, he would immediately abandon it without regret; and then study it carefully to seek other new theories.

The Chrysanthemums Have Bloomed 197

— Cai

West Wind: Let me blow!

Autumn Rain: Let me fall!

White Frost: Let me beat!

All the Flowers: Oh no! Not good!

Let's run away quickly!

We are originally heroic generals,

We are not afraid of anyone!

Two Bricks 198

— Dan Yun

Two bricks, fired together in the kiln, sat side by side, talking intimately.

Two days later, the two bricks were loaded onto a truck and transported to a construction site.

Once the house was built, one brick was placed at the highest point of the wall, while the other was placed at the base of the wall. The brick above was very proud and often mocked the one below.

"Now you are under my feet. Being above is such glory, so delightful!" it said.

"Don't be so proud. Perhaps an even worse fate awaits you," the brick below cautioned.

"Impossible, absolutely impossible."

One night, a great wind and rain caused the house to collapse. The brick above shattered as it fell, while the brick below remained standing, unshaken.

Squeezing Oil Dregs 199

— Zhu Ming

I remember when I was seven or eight years old, I went to my maternal grandparents' house and played a game called "Squeezing Oil Dregs" with many cousins and neighboring children. We would all line up on a long bench, shout "One, two, three," and then push each other with all our might. The side that had more people squeezed off would lose. Although I was very young at the time, I was also clever. I thought that sitting in the middle would make it difficult to be squeezed out. Little did I know that my strength was too weak to resist, and I was attacked from both sides, squeezed until I could barely breathe. I was completely fooled. Later, I thought it would be best to sit at the end of the bench, so I wouldn't be trapped like that. Luckily, the end I was sitting on was winning, but it wasn't because of my strength; I was just taking advantage of the situation to push along. As soon as there was an empty space at the end of the bench, those who were being squeezed on the other side rushed to this end, and I was once again squeezed into the middle, suffering the same predicament as before. So, I had no choice but to quit and dare not participate again.

Now, recalling this game, it's truly a good lesson. You must have the ability yourself to prevail in everything. If you try to be opportunistic, take advantage, or rely on others, not only is it unreliable, but it will also only bring you trouble.

When working in society, you must have the ability to be competent. Otherwise, you will be like oil dregs being squeezed out. Children, you must cultivate your abilities well to lay a solid foundation for your future work, so you won't be squeezed out!

Seven Years Old and Two Years Old 200

— Yi An

American Children's Battleship 201

— Xi Dan

Children! When you see this title, you must think it's strange. It's called the American Children's Battleship. The story of it is very admirable.

The story begins with a teacher in an elementary school in America. One day, he took many students to play by the sea. Suddenly, a warship came, moving quickly on the sea. A lively child asked, "How much does it cost to build such a warship, teacher?" The teacher replied, "A warship costs several hundred thousand dollars. But if you save the money you spend on candy and toys every day, it wouldn't be difficult to build a warship!" So, from that day on, they saved all the money they would have spent on candy and toys. Many American children joined in. Later, they actually achieved their goal. Ah! This is such a glorious thing!

Children: We hope that in the future, we can also build a Chinese Children's Battleship even bigger than the American one. This is not difficult either. As long as many children in Shanghai save all the money they would have spent on candy and toys, they will also achieve their goal in the future. So, we hope that starting today, you will quickly put it into practice.

Touch 202

— Dun

Whenever our bodies come into contact with something, we have a sensation. This sensation is touch. Touch is a strange thing. Touch nerves in our bodies also differ in sensitivity.

The most sensitive parts of the body are the fingers, lips, and tongue. If we close our eyes and want to distinguish the size and shape of an object, we must use our hands to touch it, especially our fingers to explore, in order to accurately discern it. If we spread our palm open and have someone place an object on it (as in Figure 1), we will definitely make a mistake. If we use our fingers to touch it, we can distinguish it clearly. But the sense of touch in our fingers can sometimes be inaccurate. If you close your eyes and press (as in Figure 2) on a small ball, you will definitely feel like you are pressing on two balls.

We use the sense of touch in our muscles to estimate the weight of objects. This experiment is also very amazing. If you (as in Figure 3) hold two very heavy objects, even if the weight of the two objects is different, it is difficult for us to distinguish which one is heavier and which one is lighter. But if you hold two light objects, you will immediately feel which one is heavier and which one is lighter. The sense of touch on the back is the dullest. If (as in Figure 4) you have two fingers touching your back, you will definitely only feel one finger.

It's even more interesting to experiment with touch using three basins of water with different temperatures. If you put one hand in hot water and the other hand in cold water, and after a minute or two, put both hands in lukewarm water at the same time, the hand that was just in hot water will feel the water is very cold, and the hand that was just in cold water will feel it's very hot.

Children, do you think this is very strange? Is it possible that the sense of touch can also play tricks? No, it's because our skin experiences different gains and losses of heat, so the temperature of our skin also often varies accordingly.

1. The way to distinguish the size of an object by touch

2. A small ball feels like two when touched.

3. Use touch to determine weight.

4. The sense of touch on the back is the dullest.

5. Experiment with temperature using touch.

Two Fables 203

— Qin Sun

Protector

There were many monkeys on a mountain who lived peacefully. But suddenly, a tiger came from somewhere and ate several of them every day, so that the number of monkeys gradually decreased. The entire monkey tribe became panicked and convened a meeting of all the monkeys on the mountain to discuss how to deal with the tiger and protect their lives. Everyone thought that the lion was more powerful than the tiger, so they invited the lion. Sure enough, from then on, the tiger dared not come again. But the monkeys continued to decrease day by day, because the lion replaced the tiger and ate the monkeys. This means: It is useless to rely on others.

Snake and Frog

A snake saw seven or eight frogs together on the road. It was very hungry and wanted to eat these frogs, but it was afraid that many frogs would unite and beat it, so it just waited quietly by the side. After a while, suddenly these frogs started fighting for some reason and scattered. Taking advantage of this good opportunity, the snake went over and ate them all one by one. See! Although they are weak things, when they are united, they can even scare a snake. What powerful, united strength!

Winter's Flora and Fauna 204

— Rong Yu

Little animals are going to sleep! The weather is getting colder and colder, the grass and flowers are withering, and many lively little animals have disappeared. The world is so lonely! These little animals, like frogs, bees, lizards, ants... Where are they all? It turns out they are all sleeping. They can't bear the cold, and they can't find food outside, so they simply take a long nap. When the spring breeze is warm and everything flourishes next year, they will wake up and get to work. This is called "hibernation."

Pine and cypress also wither. Pine and cypress trees have green leaves all year round, so they are called "evergreen trees." The ancients also had the saying "pine and cypress wither last." Many children doubt that the leaves of pine and cypress will not wither. In fact, that's not true. Before the old leaves fall off, new leaves have already grown. Because of metabolism, they will never be bald.

Can fish freeze to death? In December, the water is so cold. Sometimes there is a thick layer of ice on the river. Many children must wonder if fish don't wear clothes and don't sit by the fire, they will definitely freeze to death. In fact, fish hide at the bottom of the river at this time and maintain a considerable temperature. Unfrozen water remains, and they can absorb the oxygen in the water, so they will definitely not freeze to death. If the ice reaches the bottom of the river and there is no water left, the fish will stiffen, and they can no longer survive in the world.

Mr. Science Performs Magic 205

— He Gongchao

Scene One: Using Candles to Perform Magic

Mr. Science is a kind-hearted old man. Today, he is going to perform magic in front of thousands of children. As soon as he comes on stage, he takes out a candlestick, puts it on a small square table, lights the candle, and takes out a tinplate trumpet from his sock pocket.

"Everyone, who can use this trumpet to blow out the candle?"

Thousands of little hands are raised at the same time, shouting in unison: "I can... I can... It's easy..."

Mr. Science points to a girl in the front row of the stage and asks her to come up.

This child goes up, picks up the trumpet, and blows at the candle in her usual way of blowing the trumpet, with the trumpet mouth facing the candle and the tube held in her lips. She blows hard, but strangely, the candle flame not only doesn't go out, but instead floats towards the trumpet mouth (see Figure 1). Then a burst of laughter erupts from the audience.

Figure 1: Wasted Effort

Mr. Science says, "The way she blew it will not extinguish the candle. When she blows, the air comes out of the tube, goes along the smooth, sloping surface of the tinplate, and comes out of the trumpet mouth, dispersing around the candle. At the same time, the air outside immediately rushes towards the trumpet mouth to fill the empty space in the middle of the trumpet mouth. When the outside air rushes over, the flame is also carried towards the trumpet mouth. Now, if you turn the trumpet upside down and blow, you can extinguish the candle."

The child follows his instructions, puts the trumpet mouth against her own mouth, and aims the tube at the candle flame. With a blow, it goes out as expected (see Figure 2).

Mr. Science says, "The way she blows now, the air enters the trumpet from the mouth, so it is concentrated. When it comes out of the tube, the flame is subjected to this force of air, so how could it not be extinguished?"

Mr. Science then takes out a plate and a light bulb. He puts some water in the plate, relights the candle that was just extinguished, and stands it upright in the plate, then covers the candle with the light bulb. Before long, the candle flame gradually dims, and as a result, it is completely extinguished.

"Do you understand why this is?" Mr. Science asks. "Air contains a kind of oxygen, which is indispensable for combustion. Because the candle is covered with a light bulb, the oxygen inside is soon used up, so the flame has to go out. But I have a way to keep the flame from going out."

As he speaks, he picks up a piece of thick cardboard and cuts it into a T shape with scissors. He relights the candle inside the light bulb. The candle soon dims and is about to go out when he puts the T-shaped cardboard in the center of the light bulb, with the same distance on both sides. Ha! The flame lights up again!

Figure 3: Sight Restored

Mr. Science says, "You see: Because this light bulb has the cardboard on it, it is divided into two parts. The hot, used air goes out from one side, and the cold, fresh air comes in continuously from the other side, so it burns again."

"How do we know that air is going in on one side and air is coming out on the other side? Let's also perform a magic trick to prove it," he says. After speaking, he picks up two small paper streamers, strikes a match, lights them, and puts them next to the T-shaped cardboard, one on each side. At this time, the flame of one paper streamer is pointing downwards, and the other is pointing upwards.

"The flame of this paper streamer is pointing downwards, proving that air is coming in from the outside; the flame of this paper streamer is pointing upwards, proving that air is coming out from the inside."

A round of applause rises from the audience. The curtain closes. (End of Scene One)

Figure 1: In Vain 206

Figure 2: A Different Method 207

Figure 3: Sight Restored 208
