Art Scene

Record of Visiting the Joint Painting and Photography Exhibition of Xu Xingzhi and Wu Yin Xian 228

— Wei Yuan

Mr. Xu Xingzhi and Wu Yinxian exhibited their recent works in painting and photography on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA for three days on the 11th, 12th, and 13th of the month. As someone who likes these two arts very much, I took the opportunity to see them twice. Now I want to leave some of the impressions left by the two visits here.

Mr. Xu's forty-odd works tell us that he pays great attention to the depiction of reality in his subject matter. Among them, the most eye-catching are "Famine Refugees" and "Unemployed," which use the bankruptcy of rural areas and the displacement of disaster victims as their themes, as well as "Evening Walk," "Passersby by the River," "Thin Horse," "Self-Portrait," and special edition "Ah Q." "Famine Refugees" can be said to fully express the tragic state of peasants who have nowhere to turn under the attack of famine. An old couple, emaciated from wandering on the hunger line, trudges on a desolate road in a desolate wilderness overgrown with weeds. The skinny child held by the old farmer, probably his dying grandson. There is a light of unavailing help in his eyes. Next to him is also a puppy that cannot bear the hunger. This kind of subject matter, this kind of background, coupled with the author's understanding of reality and months of long-term hard work, this painting is suitable for having a deeply touching power. Especially that dog, I think it is even more indispensable in increasing the expressiveness of this painting. At the time of appreciation, I thought that if the old farmer was willing to abandon the child he was holding, the dog would immediately bite him. And now there are many facts of wild dogs eating people in the countryside.

"Unemployed" depicts a miserable posture of an unemployed person leaning dejectedly on the stone steps in front of a foreign house thinking wildly. "Evening Walk" writes about the leisure of leisurely people walking their dogs in the evening. "Passersby by the River" writes about the hard work of road workers laying roads with gravel by the river. "Thin Horse" writes about the thinness and pity of a hungry horse. These paintings can mostly arouse the attention of ordinary people, and I also think they are relatively successful works in this exhibition. As for the "Ah Q" painting, I originally had high hopes for it, but the result made me feel that it was not as good as I expected. This is naturally related to the painting time, but painting "Ah Q" into such an old, stupid, and low-energy appearance does not seem to be in line with Mr. Lu Xun's ideal "Ah Q." In terms of the composition, color scheme, and brushwork of the painting, it also does not seem to be as good as Mr. Xu's other works.

In addition, Mr. Xu's three stage designs are also worth mentioning.

Among Mr. Wu Yinxian's photography exhibition, my favorite ones are probably the following: "Relief," "Porter," "Burden Bearer," "Water Lily," "Morning Market," "Woman Drawing Water," "Terror," "Looking Up," "Before the Window," "Card Game," "Perspective," "Returning Late," etc. Among them, "Porter," "Burden Bearer," "Morning Market," "Card Game"...etc., can forcefully express the object that the author wants to express. "Looking Up" and "Before the Window" have technical success in the capture of shadow and real objects. "Woman Drawing Water" has very suitable contours and light. The rest such as "Water Lily," "Human Body" have technical success. "Woman Drawing Water" has very suitable contours and light. The rest such as "Water Lily," "Human Body," "Morning Tide," "Perspective," "Dream," "Returning Late"...etc. all have considerable achievements in photography technology.

In addition, if "Noblewoman," "Leaning," "Waiting for a Kiss," "Musing"...etc., these are relatively less impressive works.

Page 23

non-material, in fact, this concept is completely the result of being misled by the old viewpoint of the erroneous mass invariance of Newtonian physics. The research of new electron physics has factually proved that electrons change mass due to motion, and Einstein's theory of relativity further theoretically explained the variability of material mass due to different motions, etc., which is one aspect of denying Newtonian principles and the other of proving the variability of mass. However, modern natural scientists, on the contrary, based on the overturned principles of Newtonian physics, that is, recognizing that the change of electron mass due to changes in position is inconsistent with the principle of mass invariance, to deny the materiality of electrons and their mass, how confused a thing this is!

Scientifically speaking, electrons are not mysterious and unknowable mysteries. It is the last particle of the material body that has been discovered today, it has electrical energy and mass, not only can such electrons explain the material view of the unity and indivisibility of material energy, and because of the variability of its mass, it also explains the non-mechanical material view of matter. Electrons, if based on what Thomson told us, it "is like a mass of gas, it can expand to fill all the space around it, and at the same time it can shrink to a very small space"; "The electron itself can be regarded as a particle, or as a wave"; and according to the fact that the mass of electrons can increase due to motion, etc., it clearly indicates that electrons are not yet the ultimate indivisible whole, and must be composed of other smaller particles, and their own is also a complex of a particle system. Because if this is not the case, then it cannot cause changes that can be large or small, can be particles or waves, nor can it absorb energy in motion and simultaneously absorb particles to increase mass and change mass. In this case, are electrons not yet able to absorb the infinite natural world that can be divided endlessly? Are not all things like atoms, both the temporary discovery of the ultimate substance, and a material entity with real mass and energy, and is variable, not a delusional empty energy group or conceptual entity? Are electrons not an incomprehensible mystery, is the decomposition of the universe reaching the world of electricity still a real world? Is not the materialistic worldview still victorious?

A Week-Long Trip Home (1) 229

— Su Gang

I have been away from my hometown for a full seven years. During these long seven years, although I have been struggling under the pressure of life, there have been times when I have felt "raising my head to gaze at the bright moon, lowering my head to think of my hometown!" Longing for one's hometown is probably something that no one can avoid, right?

As luck would have it, just as I was being tormented by "homesickness," a letter stamped with my hometown's post office suddenly appeared before my eyes. At that moment, I, a "wild child" (Note: Someone who doesn't return home for five years is considered a wild child who has forgotten their family) banished by my hometown, was as moved as if I had seen a relative. It was simply an unexpected gain.

At this moment, my emotions were incredibly tense. The vanished scenes of my hometown surged back into my mind, and I couldn't wait to read the letter from beginning to end. However, the content of the letter did not satisfy me as much as I had anticipated. Besides reporting some trivial household matters, it expressed the hope that I would return home for a visit during this time of "local peace."

Yes, in the few years since I left my hometown, my family has lived a life of hardship and fear almost every day. Taking advantage of this "local peace," I should also go back to give them some comfort!

On the evening I received the letter, I decided on my itinerary. In the afternoon of the third day, the riverboat I was on arrived at the Jiujiang wharf.

I didn't linger long in Jiujiang. The next morning, I took the Nanchang-Xunyang Railway train to Nanchang first. After spending a night in Nanchang, I got up early the next morning and busily called the waiter to pack my luggage. However, the waiter was being difficult. I called out several times, "Waiter! Waiter!" but no one came. I looked at my watch and saw that it was almost eight o'clock, and I couldn't help but get even more anxious. So, I angrily ran out and hailed a car, loaded my luggage onto it, and told the driver to take me to Zhangjiang Gate to catch a small steamer.

Just as I was about to leave, the owner of the inn hurriedly came to meet me, asking me urgently, "Are you going to Shangrao? There are no more small steamers!"

"No more?"

"Yes! There haven't been any for a long time..."

"What should I do then?"

"There are still boats going, but they're slower," he said. Then he added, "This boat is actually quite fast, but it won't be leaving for a while!"

"There's a boat? Why isn't it leaving now?" I jumped out of the car.

"You see! It's not cost-effective for this kind of boat to rely on passengers. I heard it won't be leaving until twelve o'clock," he said with seemingly great certainty. (To be continued)

The Virgin's Heartstrings

A girl is eighteen, a bud waiting to bloom, a lotus rising from the water, lively and innocent, a lovely girl of the human world, traveling through mountains and waters, picking fruits and climbing flowers, laughing joyfully from morning to night, happy without end. A young man lures her, shy and charming, love sprouts and blossoms, a kiss on the cherry lips, her soul flies away, a tight embrace, both joyful and afraid, her heart beats wildly, she is intoxicated, a few pieces of silk, a bouquet of fresh flowers, how extravagant, let him boast, soul and body, sold to him, so-called marriage, all lies, in reality he is someone else's father, after a long time he gets tired of it, of course he changes, separation to join the army, simply deceiving her, a fool in a daze, like a papaya, crying and laughing, a storm of tears, contemplating and dreaming, he is dead, right? Sacrificing himself for the country, how can she blame him, even if the seas run dry and the rocks crumble, she will wait for him to return home, the clock on the wall, ticking away the seconds, crushing her fragrant heart, uneasy.

Storytelling with Stringed Instruments 232

Yao Xiao'an Pang Xueqing Pearl Pagoda

Zhongxi (1040) 10:00 AM - 11:00 AM

Opening "Admonition Against Smoking"

I urge you to quickly give up the opium pipe. If you give up the opium pipe, the country will become strong. Yellow face and thin body, what a misery. Hunched back and bent waist, looking unseemly. Picking paste and secretly smoking, you still violate the criminal law. Thinking about the strict prohibition of opium everywhere. The best thing is to come to Shanghai. Still blowing smoke and enjoying yourself. Opium dens are everywhere with old brands. Secret earth business is booming. Indeed, the world is separated by yin and yang. Although it is good to be carefree for now. Before long the black luck will end and the national fortune will flourish. Why not seize this opportunity to harden your heart. Do not say that the ten-mile foreign concession opens the ban. You should see how the opium business ended back then. Several lotteries were closed down. A swift and thorough cleaning. Even if it is a return of light to prolong the last breath. It is no more than three or two years and cannot last long. Thinking about the old facts of the Republic of China. It is not like the old-fashioned government documents of the former Qing Dynasty. I urge you to quickly give up the opium pipe.

Huamei (1060) 10:15 PM - 11:00 PM

"Man Jiang Hong"

After Li Taozhi finished her performance, she returned home and lay on the bed, crying with her head covered. The madam was very surprised and asked her why she was so sad. Taozhi only cried and did not answer. She knew that Director Hong would definitely come, so she pretended to be sick in bed and did not get up. After a while, Director Hong did indeed come, bringing many silk fabrics to please Taozhi. Who knew that Taozhi would not get up in bed? Director Hong felt bored and left after a while, but after Director Hong left, Taozhi's illness was also cured.

Radio News 234

Dunben Radio Station at No. 1 Zilai Village, Minguo Road, officially opened a few days ago and broadcast a special program for two days. Due to the small address and inadequate hospitality, we would like to express our gratitude and apologies to people from all walks of life, broadcasting groups, and amateur groups.

Yiyin Society is an amateur singing group, recruiting male and female members. Anyone who loves music and singing, regardless of their level, as long as they have good moral character, can register. The address is Anrun Road, Zhonghua Road, Xiaoximen. The Shanghai Starlight Society has been established for only a few days, and several major companies have entrusted it with broadcasting programs and signing contracts. Therefore, the society has a feeling of being overwhelmed in terms of female members. According to the person in charge of the society, several female members are now being recruited. Anyone who is interested in studying singing and has an interest in broadcasting can contact the society's internal affairs team directly from now until the end of this month. Those who love to sing, please do not miss this good opportunity. The address is No. 29 Foch Road, French Concession, telephone number 80496, time from 11:00 AM to 9:00 PM.
